<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the splitter&#x27;s API with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Splitter.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSplitterContext</code> hook. This lets you resize panels
programmatically:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="vertical" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#vertical"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Vertical</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">By default, the Splitter component is horizontal. If you need a vertical splitter, use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">orientation</code> prop:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="collapsible-panels" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#collapsible-panels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Collapsible Panels</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To make a panel collapsible, set the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapsible</code> prop to <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">true</code> on the panel you want to make collapsible.
Additionally, you can use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapsedSize</code> prop to set the size of the panel when it&#x27;s collapsed.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This can be useful for building sidebar layouts.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="multiple-panels" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#multiple-panels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Multiple Panels</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Here&#x27;s an example of how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Splitter</code> component with multiple panels.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_95hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the splitter is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useSplitter</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9bhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="resize-indicator" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#resize-indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Resize Indicator</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Splitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator</code> component to show a visual indicator on the resize handle.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9hhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="dynamic-collapsible" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dynamic-collapsible"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dynamic Collapsible</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapsePanel()</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">expandPanel()</code> methods to programmatically control panel collapse based on viewport size.
This is useful for responsive sidebar layouts that collapse on smaller screens.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9nhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>
<h3 id="props" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#props"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Props</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">Root</h3><p class="text c_fg.muted">Renders a <code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">&lt;div&gt;</code> element.</p><div <h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>

| &quot;vertical&quot;</code><p class="text">The orientation of the splitter.</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">getSizes</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">() =&gt; <h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>

id=\"b\"\u003eB\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n\u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Context\n\nAccess the splitter's API with `Splitter.Context` or the `useSplitterContext` hook. This lets you resize panels\nprogrammatically:\n\n**Example: context**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/react/splitter'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSplitter.Root className={styles.Root} panels={[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]}\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Context\u003e\n      {(splitter) =\u003e (\n        \u003c\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={button.Root} type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e splitter.resizePanel('a', 10)}\u003e\n              Set to 10%\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger className={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n            \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator className={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n          \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={button.Root} type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e splitter.resizePanel('b', 10)}\u003e\n              Set to 10%\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n        \u003c/\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Splitter.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/solid/splitter'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const Context = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSplitter.Root class={styles.Root} panels={[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]}\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Context\u003e\n      {(splitter) =\u003e (\n        \u003c\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n            \u003cbutton class={button.Root} type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e splitter().resizePanel('a', 10)}\u003e\n              Set to 10%\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n            \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n          \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n            \u003cbutton class={button.Root} type=\"button\" onClick={() =\u003e splitter().resizePanel('b', 10)}\u003e\n              Set to 10%\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n        \u003c/\u003e\n      )}\n    \u003c/Splitter.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/vue/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :panels=\"[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]\"\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Context v-slot=\"splitter\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"a\"\u003e\n        \u003cbutton @click=\"splitter.resizePanel('a', 10)\"\u003eSet A to 10%\u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator :class=\"styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"b\"\u003e\n        \u003cbutton @click=\"splitter.resizePanel('b', 10)\"\u003eSet B to 10%\u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.Context\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/svelte/splitter'\n  import styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSplitter.Root class={styles.Root} panels={[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]}\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.Context\u003e\n    {#snippet render(splitter)}\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onclick={() =\u003e splitter().resizePanel('a', 10)}\u003eSet to 10%\u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n        \u003cbutton type=\"button\" onclick={() =\u003e splitter().resizePanel('b', 10)}\u003eSet to 10%\u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/Splitter.Context\u003e\n\u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Vertical\n\nBy default, the Splitter component is horizontal. If you need a vertical splitter, use the `orientation` prop:\n\n**Example: vertical**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/react/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSplitter.Root className={styles.Root} orientation=\"vertical\" panels={[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]}\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n      A\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger className={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator className={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n      B\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/solid/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const Vertical = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSplitter.Root class={styles.Root} orientation=\"vertical\" panels={[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]}\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n      A\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n      B\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/vue/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" orientation=\"vertical\" :panels=\"[{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }]\"\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"a\"\u003eA\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/svelte/splitter'\n  import styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSplitter.Root \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n panel collapsible, set the `collapsible` prop to `true` on the panel you want to make collapsible.\nAdditionally, you can use the `collapsedSize` prop to set the size of the panel when it's collapsed.\n\n\u003e This can be useful for building sidebar layouts.\n\n**Example: collapsible**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/react/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const Collapsible = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSplitter.Root\n    className={styles.Root}\n    defaultSize={[15, 20]}\n    panels={[\n      { id: 'a', collapsible: true, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 10, maxSize: 20 },\n      { id: 'b', minSize: 50 },\n    ]}\n  \u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n      A\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger className={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator className={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n      B\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/solid/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const Collapsible = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cSplitter.Root\n    class={styles.Root}\n    defaultSize={[15, 20]}\n    panels={[\n      { id: 'a', collapsible: true, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 10, maxSize: 20 },\n      { id: class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n      B\n    \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/vue/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.Root\n    :class=\"styles.Root\"\n    :default-size=\"[15, 20]\"\n    :panels=\"[\n      { id: 'a', collapsible: true, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 10, maxSize: 20 },\n      { id: 'b', minSize: 50 },\n    ]\"\n  \u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"a\"\u003eA\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator :class=\"styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"b\"\u003eB\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/svelte/splitter'\n  import styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cSplitter.Root\n  class={styles.Root}\n  defaultSize={[15, 20]}\n  panels={[\n    { id: 'a', collapsible: true, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 10, maxSize: 20 },\n    { id: 'b', minSize: 50 },\n  ]}\n\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003eA\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n  \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003eB\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n\u003c/Splitter.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Multiple Panels\n\nHere's an example of how to use the `Splitter` component with multiple panels.\n\n**Example: multiple-panels**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter } from '@ark-ui/react/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const MultiplePanels = () =\u003e (\n `useSplitter` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter, useSplitter } from '@ark-ui/react/splitter'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const splitter = useSplitter({\n    defaultSize: [50, 50],\n    panels: [{ id: 'a' }, { id: 'b' }],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003coutput\u003ecurrent size: {JSON.stringify(splitter.getSizes())}\u003c/output\u003e\n\n      \u003cSplitter.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={splitter}\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n          A\n        \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger className={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize\"\u003e\n          \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator className={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n          B\n        \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter, useSplitter } from '@ark-ui/solid/splitter'\nimport styles from methods to programmatically control panel collapse based on viewport size.\nThis is useful for responsive sidebar layouts that collapse on smaller screens.\n\n**Example: dynamic-collapsible**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\n/** biome-ignore-all lint/correctness/useExhaustiveDependencies: intentional */\n\nimport { Splitter, useSplitter } from '@ark-ui/react/splitter'\nimport { useLayoutEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const DynamicCollapsible = () =\u003e {\n  const [rootSize, setRootSize] = useState\u003cnumber | null\u003e(null)\n  const ref = useRef\u003cHTMLDivElement\u003e(null)\n\n  useLayoutEffect(() =\u003e {\n    const handleResize = () =\u003e setRootSize(ref.current?.offsetWidth ?? null)\n    handleResize()\n    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n    return () =\u003e window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n  }, [])\n\n  const isBelowMd = rootSize != null \u0026\u0026 rootSize \u003c 600\n\n  useLayoutEffect(() =\u003e {\n    if (isBelowMd) splitter.collapsePanel('a')\n    else splitter.expandPanel('a')\n  }, [isBelowMd])\n\n  const splitter = useSplitter({\n    panels: [{ id: 'a', collapsible: isBelowMd, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 20, maxSize: 40 }, { id: 'b' }],\n    defaultSize: [15, 85],\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cSplitter.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={splitter} ref={ref}\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n        A\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger className={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize panels\"\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator className={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel className={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n        B\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Splitter, useSplitter } from '@ark-ui/solid/splitter'\nimport { createEffect, createSignal, onMount } from 'solid-js'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nexport const DynamicCollapsible = () =\u003e {\n  const [rootSize, setRootSize] = createSignal\u003cnumber | null\u003e(null)\n  let ref: HTMLDivElement | undefined\n\n  onMount(() =\u003e {\n    const handleResize = () =\u003e setRootSize(ref?.offsetWidth ?? null)\n    handleResize()\n    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n    return () =\u003e window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n  })\n\n  const isBelowMd = () =\u003e rootSize() != null \u0026\u0026 rootSize()! \u003c 600\n\n  const splitter = useSplitter(() =\u003e ({\n    panels: [{ id: 'a', collapsible: isBelowMd(), collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 20, maxSize: 40 }, { id: 'b' }],\n    defaultSize: [15, 85],\n  }))\n\n  createEffect(() =\u003e {\n    if (isBelowMd()) splitter().collapsePanel('a')\n    else splitter().expandPanel('a')\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cSplitter.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={splitter} ref={(el) =\u003e (ref = el)}\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003e\n        A\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize panels\"\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator class={styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator} /\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"b\"\u003e\n        B\n      \u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Splitter, useSplitter } from '@ark-ui/vue/splitter'\nimport { ref, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted, computed } from 'vue'\nimport styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\nconst rootRef = ref\u003cHTMLDivElement | null\u003e(null)\nconst rootSize = ref\u003cnumber | null\u003e(null)\n\nconst isBelowMd = computed(() =\u003e rootSize.value != null \u0026\u0026 rootSize.value \u003c 600)\n\nconst splitterProps = computed(() =\u003e ({\n  panels: [{ id: 'a', collapsible: isBelowMd.value, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 20, maxSize: 40 }, { id: 'b' }],\n  defaultSize: [15, 85],\n}))\n\nconst splitter = useSplitter(splitterProps)\n\nconst handleResize = () =\u003e {\n  rootSize.value = rootRef.value?.offsetWidth ?? null\n}\n\nonMounted(() =\u003e {\n  handleResize()\n  window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n})\n\nonUnmounted(() =\u003e {\n  window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n})\n\nwatch(isBelowMd, (below) =\u003e {\n  if (below) splitter.value.collapsePanel('a')\n  else splitter.value.expandPanel('a')\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cdiv ref=\"rootRef\" style=\"width: 100%\"\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"splitter\"\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"a\"\u003eA\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger :class=\"styles.ResizeTrigger\" id=\"a:b\" aria-label=\"Resize panels\"\u003e\n        \u003cSplitter.ResizeTriggerIndicator :class=\"styles.ResizeTriggerIndicator\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Splitter.ResizeTrigger\u003e\n      \u003cSplitter.Panel :class=\"styles.Panel\" id=\"b\"\u003eB\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003c/Splitter.RootProvider\u003e\n  \u003c/div\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Splitter, useSplitter } from '@ark-ui/svelte/splitter'\n  import { onMount } from 'svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/splitter.module.css'\n\n  let rootRef: HTMLDivElement\n  let rootSize = $state\u003cnumber | null\u003e(null)\n\n  const isBelowMd = $derived(rootSize != null \u0026\u0026 rootSize \u003c 600)\n\n  const splitter = useSplitter(() =\u003e ({\n    panels: [{ id: 'a', collapsible: isBelowMd, collapsedSize: 5, minSize: 20, maxSize: 40 }, { id: 'b' }],\n    defaultSize: [15, 85],\n  }))\n\n  $effect(() =\u003e {\n    if (isBelowMd) splitter().collapsePanel('a')\n    else splitter().expandPanel('a')\n  })\n\n  onMount(() =\u003e {\n    const handleResize = () =\u003e {\n      rootSize = rootRef?.offsetWidth ?? null\n    }\n    handleResize()\n    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n    return () =\u003e window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize)\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cdiv bind:this={rootRef} style=\"width: 100%\"\u003e\n  \u003cSplitter.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={splitter}\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.Panel class={styles.Panel} id=\"a\"\u003eA\u003c/Splitter.Panel\u003e\n    \u003cSplitter.ResizeTrigger class={styles.ResizeTrigger} id=\"a:b\"
